NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
TO WHOMSOEVER IT MAY CONCERN
Pastor Geoffrey Sam Peter the Chief Pastor of the Pentecostal Mission has expired on 22nd July 2015.
In pursuance of the Resolution No. LXXII b/2015-2016 the Deputy Chief Pastor, Pastor Stephen Natarajan has succeeded
him as the Chief Pastor on the same date as per the Nomination, dated 5th August 2015.
Pastor Stephen Natarajan will hereafter be the President cum Treasurer of the Society and the Chief Pastor of the
Mission in India. Australia, Canada, Colombia, Congo, Costa Rica, Cyprus, Dominican Republic El Salvador, Fiji, France,
Gambia, Germany, Ghana, Guadeloupe, Gulf Countries, Honduras, Hong Kong, Jamaica, Kenya, Malawi, Malaysia,
Mauritius, Mexico, Nepal, New Zealand, Nicaragua, Nigeria, Philippines, P.N.G. Puerto Rico, Seychelles, Sierra Leone,
Singapore, Sri Lanka, Switzerland, Togo, Trinidad & Tobago, U.K., U.S.A., and in any other countries wherever the work
May be extended.
Chennai-600 063
19th August 2015.

PASTOR STEPHEN K,
Assistant Secretary,
The Pentecostal Mission.

PRINTED AND PUBLISHED BY THE DIRECTOR OF STATIONERY AND PRINTING, CHENNAI
ON BEHALF OF THE GOVERNMENT OF TAMIL NADU
